Load Data\n    log(f\"Loading: {INPUT_FILE}\")\n    if not os.path.exists(INPUT_FILE):\n        log(\"ERROR: Input file not found!\")\n        return\n        \n    df = pd.read_excel(INPUT_FILE)\n    log(f\"Rows loaded: {len(df)}\")\n\n    # 2. Identify Address Column\n    addr_col = \"FullAddress2\" if \"FullAddress2\" in df.columns else \"FullAddress\"\n    log(f\"Using address column: {addr_col}\")\n\n    # 3. Prepare Unique Addresses\n    # We rename to 'Address' to ensure simple mapping\n    unique_df = pd.DataFrame({'Address': df[addr_col].unique()})\n    unique_df = unique_df.dropna()\n    log(f\"Unique addresses to geocode: {len(unique_df)}\")\n    \n    unique_df.to_csv(TEMP_CSV, index=False)\n    \n    # 4. Run Geocoding\n    log(\"Starting GeocodeAddresses (ArcPy)...\")\n    out_fc = \"memory/dec_geocoded\"\n    \n    # Mapping for NJ Locator: \"Address OR Intersection\"\n    # We map the CSV column 'Address' to the locator field 'Address'\n    # Format: \"LocatorField InputColumn VISIBLE NONE\"\n    field_map = \"Address Address VISIBLE NONE\"\n    \n    try:\n        arcpy.geocoding.GeocodeAddresses(\n            in_table=TEMP_CSV,\n            address_locator=LOCATOR,\n            in_address_fields=field_map,\n            out_feature_class=out_fc\n        )\n        log(\"Geocoding complete.\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        log(f\"CRITICAL GEOCODING ERROR: {e}\")\n        return\n\n    # 5. Extract Results\n    log(\"Extracting coordinates...\")\n    \n    # List fields to find the correct input address field in output\n    # Usually it's 'USER_Address' or just 'Address' depending on CSV\n    fields = [f.name for f in arcpy.ListFields(out_fc)]\n    input_addr_field = \"USER_Address\" if \"USER_Address\" in fields else \"Address\"\n    \n    results = []\n    # Read X, Y, and the Input Address to join back\n    with arcpy.da.SearchCursor(out_fc, [input_addr_field, \"SHAPE@X\", \"SHAPE@Y\"]) as cursor:\n        for row in cursor:\n            results.append({\n                'Address': row[0],\n                'X_Coord': row[1],\n                'Y_Coord': row[2]\n            })\n            \n    result_df = pd.DataFrame(results)\n    log(f\"Extracted {len(result_df)} geocoded records.\")\n\n    # 6. Merge Back\n    log(\"Merging results...\")\n    # Join the geocoded results (result_df) back to the original unique list (unique_df)\n    # Then merge that back to the main dataframe (df)\n    \n    # First, join coords to the unique list to ensure 1-to-1\n    # Note: result_df has 'Address', 'X_Coord', 'Y_Coord'\n    \n    final_df = df.merge(result_df, left_on=addr_col, right_on='Address', how='left')\n    \n    # Clean up duplicate address column from merge if needed\n    if 'Address' in final_df.columns and addr_col != 'Address':\n        del final_df['Address']\n\n    # 7. Check if ArcGIS recognizes this as a spatial layer or just a table\n    # BaseDataType will be 'FeatureClass' if it has points, 'Table' if it doesn't\n    data_type = desc.dataType\n    shape_type = getattr(desc, \"shapeType\", \"N/A (No Geometry)\")\n    \n    # Check the Coordinate System\n    sr = desc.spatialReference\n    sr_name = sr.name if sr else \"Unknown\"\n    \n    # Count how many records actually have a physical point object\n    actual_points = 0\n    total_records = int(arcpy.management.GetCount(path)[0])\n    \n    # A. Carucci\n# Purpose: Pull daily data, geocode missing points, and push spatial features to dashboard\n\nimport arcpy\nimport os\nimport sys\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# ============================================================================\n# CONFIGURATION\n# ============================================================================\nINPUT_EXCEL = r\"C:\\HPD ESRI\\03_Data\\CAD\\Backfill\\_STAGING\\ESRI_CADExport.xlsx\\Sheet1$\"\nGDB = r\"C:\\HPD ESRI\\LawEnforcementDataManagement_New\\LawEnforcementDataManagement.gdb\"\nFINAL_FC = os.path.join(GDB, \"CFStable\") # MUST BE A FEATURE CLASS\nONLINE_SERVICE = \"https://services1.arcgis.com/JYl0Hy0wQdiiV0qh/arcgis/rest/services/CallsForService_2153d1ef33a0414291a8eb54b938507b/FeatureServer/0\"\nNJ_LOCATOR = \"https://geodata.mdt.nj.gov/arcgis/rest/services/Geocoders/ATLAS_Roads_Address_Locator/GeocodeServer\"\n\n# Temporary Workspace\nTEMP_TABLE = os.path.join(GDB, \"temp_daily_table\")\nTEMP_GEOCODED = os.path.join(GDB, \"temp_daily_geocoded\")\n\ndef log(msg):\n    print(f\"[{datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')}] {msg}\")\n\ndef main():\n    try:\n        log(\"Starting Daily Geocoding & Publish...\")\n\n        # 1. Clean up old temps\n        for item in [TEMP_TABLE, TEMP_GEOCODED]:\n            if arcpy.Exists(item): arcpy.management.Delete(item)\n\n        # 2. Import Excel to Table\n        arcpy.conversion.ExcelToTable(INPUT_EXCEL, TEMP_TABLE)\n        \n        # 3. RUN NJ GEOCODER\n        log(\"Geocoding addresses with NJ State Locator...\")\n        arcpy.geocoding.GeocodeAddresses(\n            in_table=TEMP_TABLE,\n            address_locator=NJ_LOCATOR,\n            in_address_fields=\"FullAddress 'FullAddress' VISIBLE NONE\",\n            out_feature_class=TEMP_GEOCODED\n        )\n\n        # 4. Clean Slate Fix: Recreate CFStable as a true FEATURE CLASS\n        log(\"Rebuilding CFStable as a spatial layer...\")\n        if arcpy.Exists(FINAL_FC): arcpy.management.Delete(FINAL_FC)\n        \n        # This creates the physical 'SHAPE' field automatically\n        arcpy.management.CopyFeatures(TEMP_GEOCODED, FINAL_FC)\n\n        # 5. Push to Online (Clearing old data first to avoid duplicates)\n        log(\"Truncating online service and uploading points...\")\n        arcpy.management.TruncateTable(ONLINE_SERVICE)\n        arcpy.management.Append(FINAL_FC, ONLINE_SERVICE, \"NO_TEST\")\n\n        log(\"✅ SUCCESS: Points are now live on the map.\")\n        return 0\n\n    except Exception as e:\n        log(f\"❌ ERROR: {e}\")\n        return 1\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    sys.exit(main())\n\n\n\nWhy this fixes the problem\n\n\nForce-Creates Shape: By using CopyFeatures instead of Append, it forces the GDB to recognize the file as a Feature Class (with map dots) instead of a flat table.\n\nAuto-Geocoding: It hits the NJ State Geocoder every morning. If the CAD export is missing coordinates, the script fills them in using the FullAddress field before uploading.\n\nNo Duplicates: It uses TruncateTable to wipe the dashboard before the new upload, preventing the \"5 copies of every record\" issue we saw in your table.\n\n\nNext Step: Replace the script, run it, and refresh your dashboard. Create Point Geometry from Excel X/Y Columns\n        log(\"Creating spatial points from longitude/latitude columns...\")\n        # We use WGS84 (4326) because the cached data is in GPS coordinates\n        spatial_ref = arcpy.SpatialReference(4326)\n        \n        temp_layer = \"temp_xy_layer\"\n        arcpy.management.MakeXYEventLayer(INPUT_EXCEL, \"longitude\", \"latitude\", temp_layer, spatial_ref)\n\n        # 2. Rebuild CFStable as a true FEATURE CLASS (Blue point icon)\n        log(\"Rebuilding local CFStable Feature Class...\")\n        if arcpy.Exists(FINAL_FC):\n            arcpy.management.Delete(FINAL_FC)\n        \n        # Copying the layer to the GDB creates the SHAPE geometry field\n        arcpy.management.CopyFeatures(temp_layer, FINAL_FC)\n\n        # 3.

Push to Online Dashboard\n        log(\"Clearing duplicates and uploading points to Dashboard...\")\n        arcpy.management.TruncateTable(ONLINE_SERVICE)\n        arcpy.management.Append(FINAL_FC, ONLINE_SERVICE, \"NO_TEST\")\n\n        log(\"✅ SUCCESS: Map points have been restored.\")\n        return 0\n\n    except Exception as e:\n        log(f\"❌ ERROR: {e}\")\n        return 1\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    sys.exit(main())\n'@\n\n$newCode | Out-File -FilePath $scriptPath -Encoding utf8 -Force\nWrite-Host \"✅ Script rewritten to use X/Y columns instead of a geocoder.\" -ForegroundColor Cyan\n\n\nStep 2: Run the Fixed Script\n\n\nRun this command in the same PowerShell window:\n\n\n& \"C:\\Program Files\\ArcGIS\\Pro\\bin\\Python\\Scripts\\propy.bat\" \"C:\\HPD ESRI\\04_Scripts\\publish_with_xy_coordinates.py\"\n\n\n\nWhy this will work\n\n\nNo External Dependencies: It doesn't need the NJ Locator or the \"World\" geocoder, so no more ERROR 000005.\n\nForces Geometry: By using MakeXYEventLayer and CopyFeatures, it forces the creation of a Feature Class (map points) instead of a flat Table (gray grid).\n\nRestores the Map: Once the upload finishes, the hidden SHAPE field will be populated, and the points will finally appear on your dashboard map.\n\n\nPlease refresh your dashboard once this completes.
